The websites and apps that you use are under attack every day. Security breaches occur and your passwords are stolen. When you reuse the same passwords across apps and websites hackers can easily access your email, bank, and other important accounts.\r\n\r\nSecurity experts recommend that you use a different, randomly generated password for every account that you create.
